Economic Discussions

China's Coal 60

— Edited by Tang Qingzeng; original work by W. Belden-M. Salter, translated by Ziming

China's coal deposits are distributed throughout the country, with the largest reserves in Shanxi and Shaanxi provinces. The reserves in other provinces are generally sufficient to meet local needs. The output of Xinjiang, Qinghai, and Gansu has not been thoroughly surveyed. In the southern provinces of mainland China, coal seams are mostly exposed on mountain sides, making local mining very easy. Chinese geologist Weng Wenhao once said, "In Yunnan, one can travel fifty miles without seeing an exposed coal seam, which is unheard of. Fujian is rich in coal production. Even the poorest families use coal day and night, as it is more economical than extinguishing and re-igniting the fire." Shanxi and Shaanxi have extremely large coal reserves but very little output. Kailuan Coal Mine, although not large in reserves, is very important due to its convenient mining and transportation.

The coal deposits in the three northeastern provinces are mostly located deep within the Changbai Mountain range, making mining very inconvenient. The most important are the Fushun, Benxi Lake, and Yantai coalfields, which are mined by the Japanese. Their output accounts for 80% of the total output of the four northeastern provinces. The total output of the Northeast in 1931 was 9,000,000 tons, with this area accounting for 7,200,000 tons. In addition, there are still unexploited reserves in Muling and Mishan in Jilin, the Hegang in Heilongjiang, and Beipiao in Rehe. The coal resources in these areas are of poor quality and cannot be used for coking, so their industrial applications are limited. The coal from Kailuan and Benxi Lake can be coked and has extensive industrial and naval applications.

Shanxi and Shaanxi have extremely large reserves of anthracite and bituminous coal, but due to inconvenient transportation and difficult transport, the mining industry is underdeveloped, resulting in very little output. It is a great pity that the goods are abandoned in the ground. The main transportation line in the area is only from the plain to Taiyuan, and the high freight costs naturally preclude its use for transporting coal. Currently, the coal mines being mined are mostly in the Fen River valley and the southeastern border connecting the North China Plain, where the population is also denser.

Fushun Coal Mine has a good location and convenient transportation. The South Manchurian Railway even has a branch line to Fushun. The mine is located on the coast, making transportation to Tianjin very convenient. Kailuan coal can now be exported through the Qinhuangdao ice-free port, making it even more convenient.

Currently, there are forty-eight modern coal mines nationwide, of which only 33% are mined with Chinese capital, 30% with Japanese capital, and 10% with British capital. Kailuan and Fushun both use modern mining methods, and the coal pits in Fushun are particularly impressive. The largest mine pit has been mined for seventy years and is now two hundred feet deep.

The coal in Shandong is of excellent quality and easy to transport. Many mines are using modern mining methods. The Zhuangzhongxing Coal Mine can be said to be a model coal mine. The monthly income of the workers in the mine ranges from 7.5 yuan to 58 yuan, which is enough to support their entire families due to the extremely low cost of living.

There are approximately 200,000 miners in China, including those working in both new and old mines. Each person can mine 0.35 tons of coal per day, which is only 126 tons per year. In comparison, Belgium produces 200 tons per person per year, the United Kingdom 225 tons, and the United States 688 tons. The efficiency of Chinese coal mines is far behind.

China has the largest coal reserves in the world. We believe that to find ways to mining, there must be four prerequisites: (1) Develop transportation infrastructure; (2) Stabilize politics and finance; (3) Develop other industries; (4) Accumulate capital and technical personnel. Attached Table 1.

Unprecedented Large-Scale Exercises by Japanese Troops Stationed in North China 65

Targeting Key Points on the Beining Railway and Tianjin City 1,200 Troops from Japanese Army in Pingjin Participate

Tianjin Dispatch: The Japanese army stationed in North China conducted a large-scale autumn exercise from the 4th, with unprecedented objectives and troop participation. It ended at 8:00 AM on the 7th. A review was held at the Tianjin East Bureau Airfield, commanded by Tada, the commander of the Japanese troops stationed in Tianjin, and directed by Hasegawa, a colonel of the Japanese army stationed in Pingjin. All veterans, volunteer corps, students, and National Defense Women's Association members participated. After the review, Tada read the Emperor's edict and held a debriefing to assess the strengths and weaknesses of the exercise. It concluded around 1:00 PM. The troops stationed in Ping left Tianjin at 4:10 PM. The troops along the Shanhaiguan and other lines left Tianjin at 2:25 PM. The participating troops in this exercise included infantry, cavalry, artillery, communications, and medical teams from Beijing, Tianjin, Tanggu, Shanhaiguan, and Tangshan, totaling over 1,200. In the exercise on the 4th, the Beijing troops were designated as the Red Army, commanded by Hasegawa, and the Tianjin troops as the Blue Army, commanded by Kayashima. Initially, the Red Army advanced south from Beijing and encountered the Blue Army from Tianjin in Langfang, resulting in an engagement. The Shanhaiguan and Tangshan troops, designated as the Blue Army, received reports and deployed a train overnight to provide assistance. They disembarked at the An Ding and Wei Shanzhuang stations. As the Red Army was advancing from Fengtai, a train carrying reinforcements arrived, leading to a major field battle between the Red and Blue armies near Wei Shanzhuang on the morning of the 5th. Around 3:00 AM on the 5th, the Red Army's reinforcements were cut off, and they gradually retreated. The Blue Army gradually gained the upper hand. By the evening of the 5th, the Red Army was overwhelmed and retreated from Huangcun. They crossed the Yongding River at night, pursued relentlessly by the Blue Army, resulting in a night battle on both sides of the river. By the morning of the 6th, the Red Army occupied the commanding heights of Changxindian on the west bank of the Yongding River, encouraging the troops for a final stand. A battle ensued in the morning, and by noon, the Red Army, with united efforts, finally defeated the Blue Army. This was the situation of the first stage of the exercise. In the afternoon of the 6th, the second stage of the exercise began. The Shanhaiguan Blue Army was assigned to attack Tianjin. In the afternoon of the 6th, a train carrying troops departed from Shanhaiguan. At that time, the Red Army was far away in Beijing and was ordered to urgently reinforce Tianjin. In the afternoon of the 6th, three trains were dispatched. Only one train passed the Luofa station before the railway bridge was blown up by the Blue Army (simulated). The soldiers on the remaining two trains disembarked locally and traveled to Tianjin by car, arriving in the vicinity of the Tianjin East Bureau successively in the evening and deploying defenses. The Blue Army's train advanced to Lutai and discovered that the railway bridge and tracks had been destroyed in advance by the Red Army. They disembarked in Tangshan and advanced towards Dongfengtai. They gathered at the Junliangcheng dormitory overnight, preparing for a dawn attack on the 7th. Tianjin felt threatened, and 69 veterans and 64 teachers and students from youth schools, along with 36 commercial school students, were temporarily organized into a volunteer corps, commanded by the director of the Veterans Association branch, Tian. They assisted in guarding the outskirts of Tianjin and dispatched a unit to enter Junliangcheng to disrupt the Blue Army's rear. The remaining troops from the Japanese Garrison in Tianjin at the Haiguang Temple, including all tanks and armored vehicles, were dispatched to Haixia, Chentangzhuang, and Zhangguizhuang, harassing the front of the Blue Army in Junliangcheng, hindering their advance. By 5:00 AM on the 7th, the Blue Army launched a full-scale attack, employing new weapons and chemical warfare tactics, with simulated skirmishes and hand-to-hand combat, using blood and flesh as projectiles. The exercise was realistic. It concluded at 8:00 AM. The victory in the Tianjin suburban defense battle belonged to the Red Army. (7th)

Wuhan Party, Government, Military, and Business Sectors Jointly Discuss Prices 66

Organize Price Evaluation Committee to Curb Excessive Inflation Provincial Bank Issues Subsidiary Coins to Address Copper Coin Shortage Legal Tender Foundation Established, Foreign Merchants Universally Use

Hankou Dispatch: After the currency reform in Wuhan, although market transactions continue as usual, commodity prices have soared, and copper coins are difficult to exchange, inevitably causing disturbances. Despite the joint efforts of officials and merchants to maintain stability in recent days, no satisfactory result has been achieved. Among foreign merchants, HSBC (British) and Citibank (American) were the first to accept legal tender, while others temporarily observed. As of today, Mercantile Bank (British), Deutsch-Asiatische Bank (German), Banque Belge pour l'Etranger (Belgian), Yokohama Specie Bank (Japanese), Bank of Taiwan (Japanese), Hankou Bank (Japanese), and Banque de l'Indochine (French) have also continued to adopt legal tender. Consequently, companies such as Méts & Co. (American), Standard Oil (American), Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company (British/Swiss), British-American Tobacco Company (British/American), Tsuda & Co. (Japanese), Toyo Cotton Company (Japanese), Nissin Trading Co. (Japanese), Mitsubishi Corporation (Japanese), Abe Trading Co. (Japanese), Kyoei Trading Co. (Japanese), Ki Lai Trading Co. (Japanese), A.S. Watson & Co. (British), Iwai & Co. (Japanese), British American Tobacco Co. (Daxie Tobacco Company), Long Mao Trading Co. (Jin Long Trading Co.), Texaco (American), De Fuyou Company (German), have followed suit, fully resuming operations. In addition to the legal tender issued by the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and Bank of China, the notes issued by the Jiangsu & Zhejiang Commercial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Commercial Bank of China, Bank of China, Farmers Bank of China, China Peasants Bank, and Hubei Provincial Bank are also circulating in the market. Outside of Wuhan, in counties and cities such as Yichang and Shashi, the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and Bank of China have branches. The shortage of copper coins is felt in Wuhan and other places, making it difficult to travel by boat or car. Yesterday, the authorities stipulated measures to deal with hoarding by foreign merchants, but they were largely ignored. Today, the Chamber of Commerce decided that the Provincial Bank would issue subsidiary coins of 100 cash to circulate throughout the province, while strictly cracking down on hoarding by unscrupulous merchants. It is reported that the Ministry of Finance will also issue one-fen copper subsidiary coins and five-fen subsidiary coins to circulate nationwide. If they can be minted soon, it may be sufficient to meet the demand. Due to speculation by unscrupulous merchants, prices of various commodities are increasing daily, and the prices of daily necessities are skyrocketing, which is currently the most serious problem. Although prices have stabilized slightly under the strict orders of the government today, it cannot be considered that the situation has been alleviated. The Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, Hankou Municipal Government, Bankers Association, Money Dealers Association, and General Chamber of Commerce held another emergency joint meeting today, deciding to organize the Wuhan Price Evaluation Committee to limit the excessive price increases in the three towns of Wuhan. The committee will be jointly organized by representatives from the Hubei Provincial Party Headquarters, Hankou Municipal Party Headquarters, Hubei Provincial Government, Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, Hankou Municipal Government, Wuhan three chambers of commerce, and the Bankers Association. Attached to the Provincial Government, it will have staff assigned by various agencies and organizations to investigate prices at any time. If the committee deems that prices are rising excessively, it may request the competent authorities to take effective measures. If it is found that there is a shortage of certain goods, it will also consult with the competent authorities and the local chamber of commerce to find ways to raise funds for procurement and make adjustments. It is expected that the committee will be established and start work tomorrow. Minister of Finance Kong expressed concern about the discount on banknotes in Hankou. On the 6th, he telegraphed Hankou Mayor Wu Guozhen and Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng, ordering them to strictly crack down on it. The telegram stated, "This unified issuance and centralized reserve is an essential plan for stabilizing finance and reviving the economy. All provinces and cities are unanimously complying. The Hankou Chamber of Commerce has already sent a reply stating that it will fully comply. It has been reported that there is a discount on banknotes in Hankou, which must be due to a few unscrupulous merchants trying to profit from the opportunity. I hope that you two will strictly investigate and prohibit it and clearly explain the situation. If anyone violates the law again, please punish them according to the law to deter others and facilitate implementation. [Seal of Kong Xiangxi]" Mayor Wu replied today, "I have received your telegram. The Money Dealers Association of this city issued a public notice on the 4th stating that the exchange rate for ten-day deferred Shanghai drafts would deduct three yuan in silver, which has been stopped and corrected. There is currently no discount on banknotes. The market situation is currently good, but the price of copper coins has risen, making small-scale trade difficult. In addition to the municipal government convening the Chamber of Commerce and money dealers to set a legal exchange rate of six strings of copper coins per yuan and prohibiting the outflow of copper coins from the urban area to provide relief, are there any other methods to adjust the situation? Please advise. It is also reported that the high price of copper coins is the same in all places. It seems that your ministry should quickly determine a subsidiary coin solution to facilitate circulation. Respectfully, Wu Guozhen, Mayor of Hankou [Seal]" (7th)

Songjiang County Government Convenes Rice Stem Borer Meeting

The county government received an instruction from the Construction Department, stating that 31 counties including Wuxi and Songjiang are infested with rice stem borers and urgent measures should be taken to eliminate them. The "Implementation Measures for the Rice Stem Borer Control Campaign Committee" were issued, ordering the county to comply. County Magistrate Li convened a meeting on the afternoon of the 9th at 2:00 PM, gathering the county party headquarters, district chiefs, the Public Security and Education Bureaus, various civil education centers, rice crop testing grounds, and other agencies to discuss the organization of the committee. It was decided that the 19 agencies, including the district chiefs, would serve as members, and the county party headquarters, county government, Public Security and Education Bureaus, and the First District Office would serve as standing committee members. The county party headquarters would be responsible for publicity, the rice crop testing ground would provide rice stem borer control methods, and the information would be widely disseminated. The county government would be responsible for general affairs, with the committee's office located in the county government. A publicity week was also set to organize a publicity team.

Suzhou Police Officer Murder Case Opened Yesterday

The case of Hong Shiqin, a patrol officer from the Fifth Precinct of the First Public Security Bureau, who incited police officer He Naikang and others to murder Gu A'gen, a incense stick seller of the Chen Family Nunnery in Guan Zai Lane, was concluded after an investigation by the District Prosecutor's Office. He was prosecuted on charges of inciting murder, intimidation, and forgery of documents. Judge Fang Huan was assigned to handle the case. During the investigation, Judge Fang became ill, and Judge Shen Bingrong took over the case. The trial was scheduled for 10:00 AM on the 9th. The defendants hired four lawyers, including Yao Xiaoqiu and Zhu Fucheng, to defend them. Judge Shen questioned each defendant separately for four hours. Judge Shen believed that the case was of great importance and required further investigation, so the trial was adjourned to a later date. The defendants were returned to custody.

Wuxi Strict Prevention of Railway Track Sabotage

The Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, in view of recent incidents where large and small stones were found on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway tracks in the Wujin section and near Anting Station, with the intention of sabotage, and the Suzhou Weiting Station and Kunshan Station, where patrolling soldiers had apprehended Jiang Duzhuang, Guangshan, Wang Wenwen, Guo Zhuang, and Chunmei in Lumu Township and Anting Station for allegedly plotting to sabotage the railway tracks in the Suzhou-Wuxi-Changzhou sections, realized that the railway and highway transportation arteries should be strictly guarded as the winter defense season approached. A police affairs meeting was convened yesterday, resolving the following: (1) All sub-bureaus and stations should be notified to conduct thorough patrols in advance and implement winter defense measures. (2) Police officers should not leave the bureau except for patrols and business trips to strengthen defense. (3) Strict attention should be paid to the protection of railways and highways at all points, in accordance with orders. (4) Any police officer who leaves the bureau without permission will be severely punished.

Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce Requests Establishment of a Reserve Sub-Treasury

The Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce convened an executive committee meeting on the evening of the 5th and decided on the following: (1) Telegraph the Ministry of Finance to request the establishment of a reserve sub-treasury in the provincial capitals and important cities. (2) Due to the contraction of currency and shortage of funds in the city, request the Central Bank, Bank of Communications, and Bank of China to provide loans to maintain the market. (3) In response to the letter from the Provincial Chamber of Commerce regarding the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce's initiative to jointly use commercial acceptance drafts, request the Bankers Association and Money Dealers Association to draft opinions for review. Regarding the implementation of the new currency policy, the Finance Department has received numerous telegrams from the province requesting clarification and has issued instructions based on the implementation measures formulated by the Provincial Government. As for the grace period, Yin County requested that it be extended to the end of December, which the Provincial Government approved.

Educational Broadcasting Supplement

How the Sun, Moon, Stars, and Planets Move and the Phenomena Resulting from Their Motions (II) (Lectures to the National Public on October 18th, 21st, 27th, and 28th) 67

— Chen Zungui, Researcher at the Institute of Astronomy, Academia Sinica

Among the nine major planets, besides the Earth, there are eight others. Of these eight, Mercury and Venus are closer to the sun than the Earth, meaning their orbits are inside the Earth's orbit. Mars through Pluto are farther from the sun than the Earth, meaning their orbits are outside the Earth's orbit. Astronomers call the planets with orbits inside the Earth's orbit "inner planets," and those outside "outer planets." The apparent motion of inner and outer planets as seen from Earth is different.

When an inner planet, the sun, and the Earth are in a straight line, it's called a conjunction. Conjunctions are divided into superior and inferior conjunctions. When an inner planet appears behind the sun, meaning the sun is between the Earth and the inner planet, it's called a superior conjunction. When an inner planet appears in front of the sun, meaning the inner planet is between the sun and the Earth, it's called an inferior conjunction. Now, please prepare a piece of paper and a pencil. Draw two concentric circles on the paper, meaning two circles of different sizes with the same center point. Assume the center is the sun, the inner circle is the orbit of an inner planet, and the outer circle is the orbit of the Earth. Pick any point on the outer circle, for example, point A. Connect point A to the sun, and it will intersect the inner circle at one point, for example, point B. If the Earth is at point A and the inner planet is at point B, this is called an inferior conjunction. If you extend the straight line between points A and B, it will intersect the inner circle at another point, for example, point C. If the Earth is at point A and the inner planet is at point C, this is called a superior conjunction. During a superior conjunction, we see it moving from west to east, which is direct motion. During an inferior conjunction, we see it moving from east to west, which is retrograde motion. Also, the orbit of an inner planet is smaller than the Earth's orbit, so the distance between them and the sun, as seen from Earth, is limited. Venus cannot exceed 46 degrees, and Mercury cannot exceed 28 degrees. Because of this, we can only see Venus and Mercury in the early morning or at dusk. Mercury is very small and its maximum distance from the sun cannot exceed 28 degrees, so it often appears and disappears around the sun, making it very difficult to observe. Venus is what we in ancient China called the Taibai Star. Its distance from the sun can reach 46 degrees, so often when the sun is about to rise, all other stars are invisible, but Venus can still be recognized in the eastern sky. In ancient China, we called it the Morning Star, which is Venus at this time. Also, when the sun has just set and other stars are invisible, only Venus shines brightly in the western sky. In ancient China, we called it the Evening Star. So, the saying "East has the Morning Star, West has the Evening Star" refers to different names for the same Venus. When the distance between Venus and the sun is 39 and a half degrees, its luminosity is greatest during inferior conjunction, meaning that Venus can be seen even during the day for about 36 days before and after its inferior conjunction. It takes about 500 days for Venus to complete one inferior conjunction cycle, so its brightest appearance may not be seen at all in a year, or it may be seen twice in a year. For example, Venus was in inferior conjunction with the sun on September 8th of this year, so it was brightest about 36 days before that, around August 3rd. At that time, newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai reported news of seeing celestial bodies during the day, which was the period when Venus could be seen during the day. Also, 36 days after September 8th, that is, on the 15th of this month, it will be brightest again. So, Venus has two periods of peak brightness this year.

The above describes the situation of the inner planets. Now, let's talk about the outer planets. When an outer planet, the sun, and the Earth are in a straight line, it's called a conjunction when the sun is between the outer planet and the Earth, and an opposition when the Earth is between the sun and the planet. Referring to the diagram drawn above, assume the inner circle is the orbit of the Earth and the outer circle is the orbit of an outer planet. This means the Earth is at point B and the outer planet is at point A. This is called opposition. Extend BC and it intersects the outer circle at point D. When the Earth is at point B and the outer planet is at point D, this is called conjunction. Outer planets mostly move from west to east, with only slight retrograde motion around opposition. The opposition of Mars is most famous in astronomy.

The above describes the motion of planets and satellites as seen from Earth. Now, fourthly, we want to talk about the motion of comets. Comets are commonly called broom stars. What we usually see are stars with long tails. They also orbit the sun, but their orbital shape is not a near-circular ellipse like planets. It is a long ellipse or even a parabola shape, or even a hyperbola shape. Comets with elliptical orbits return once at a certain period, which is called a periodic comet. For example, in the second year of Xuantong (1910 AD), we saw a very large star with a long tail, which is called Halley's Comet. Its orbit is elliptical, and it orbits the sun about every 76 years, so we can predict in advance that this comet will reappear in 1986. There were also records of comets appearing in the 15th year of Daoguang (1835 AD), the 24th year of Qianlong (1759 AD), and the 25th year of Kangxi (1682 AD). These comets are also returns of Halley's Comet. If we go further back, we can know that the earliest historical record of the appearance of this comet was in the seventh year of Qin Shihuang (240 BC). Since then, it has returned 29 times. Before the development of human science, it was believed that the appearance of a comet meant that some disaster was about to happen. Most strangely, after the appearance of Halley's Comet in the second year of Xuantong, the Qing Dynasty ended. The people at that time were still superstitious. Now, according to historical records and the observations and calculations of astronomers, it has been clearly proven that this is the motion of a comet. We can not only know the past appearances of comets, but also predict future appearances, so superstitious ideas have naturally been broken.

Fifth, is meteors. We often see points of light flying across the sky at night, which are meteors. Although meteors are tiny dust particles in the universe, their motion is not random. They often form groups and orbit the sun, mostly following the orbits of comets. Sometimes comets disappear after several orbits, but the meteors orbiting along its orbit continue to be observed, so we can also say that meteors are the remains of comets. Meteoroids are at different distances from the sun, so their orbital speeds are also different. Thus, they gradually distribute themselves along the orbit. The longer the time, the longer the orbit, resulting in a long elliptical ring of dust. Because of the relationship between these elliptical orbits and the Earth's orbit, certain groups of meteors appear on certain dates each year.

In short, in the solar system, except for satellites that orbit planets, all celestial bodies revolve around the sun as the center. So, the sun is the master of the solar system. As for why the stars orbit the sun and why their orbits are elliptical, this has to do with the effect of universal gravitation. It's a bit specialized, so we won't talk about it for now. Now we want to talk about the motion of the fixed star sphere.

We have already said above that the positions of fixed stars are permanently fixed, but upon detailed study, they are absolutely not fixed. They also change, but they are so far away from us that it's not easy to detect with our eyes. The arrangement of the stars in the sky changes naturally after a certain number of years, but the change is very small. For example, take the Big Dipper. What is the Big Dipper? Everyone knows that when we look north at night, there are seven bright stars arranged in the shape of an iron. That's the Big Dipper. The position we see now is three stars in the handle and four stars in the ladle. Now, please prepare another piece of paper and a pencil, and draw the shape of the Big Dipper on the paper, with the mouth of the ladle facing up and the bottom of the ladle horizontal. Each star has a name, starting from the first star at the end of the handle, called Yaoguang, Kaiyang, Yuheng, Tianquan, Tianji, Tianxuan, and Tianxu. These are astronomical names. Now, for convenience, let's temporarily use 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, and 7 as their names. Connect them with lines in order, and their current position is 1 and 2 parallel to the bottom of the ladle, forming a horizontal direction. 2, 3, and 4 are almost in a straight line, slightly to the lower right. Also, the lengths of 1-2, 2-3, and 3-4 are almost the same. 4-5 folds further to the lower right. 5-6 is the bottom, and 6-7 folds back to the upper right. Its length is about the same as 4-5. You can tell this shape by looking at the sky.

But 200,000 years ago and 200,000 years later, their positions will be completely different. Now, let's talk about 200,000 years ago. Their shape at that time was that the four stars in the handle, 1, 2, 3, and 4, were almost in a straight line, and the length of 1-2 was longer than the combined length of 2-3 and 3-4. 4-5, compared to 5-6, did not fold upwards to the left as it does now, but slightly upwards to the right. 6-7 folded diagonally upwards to the left, meaning that the mouth of the ladle was wide at the top and narrow at the bottom. At that time, the mouth of the ladle was narrow at the top and wide at the bottom, and the diameter of the mouth was almost only half the length of the bottom. Also, the length of 6-7 was half longer than that of 4-5. Now let's talk about the shape 200,000 years later. At that time, 1-2 will not be horizontal, meaning it will not be parallel to the bottom of the ladle, but in a direction perpendicular to the bottom of the ladle. 6-7 will be diagonally to the right, but slightly above the bottom edge, meaning one side of the ladle will move outward, and the long diameter of the mouth of the ladle will be more than twice the length of the bottom edge. Looking at it this way, 200,000 years ago or 200,000 years later, we definitely cannot call these seven stars the Big Dipper anymore, because their shape is no longer a dipper shape at all.

Central Trust Bureau to Establish Special Department for Real Estate Mortgage Loans 77

Preparatory Committee for Issuance to Hold Second General Meeting; Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notifies That All Negotiable Instruments Must Be Written in National Currency

Following the Ministry of Finance's announcement that the notes of the Central, China, and Communications Banks are legal tender, the Central Trust Bureau will establish a special department for real estate mortgage loans to invigorate the real estate market. The Preparatory Committee for Issuance will hold its first general meeting to approve procedural rules and discuss all matters related to the operation. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce has announced that all negotiable instruments must be written using the term "National Currency." Details are as follows:

Preparatory Committee to Hold General Meeting

After the establishment of the Issuance Preparatory Management Committee to manage the reserve funds for legal tender and handle the issuance and exchange of legal tender, in addition to dispatching committee members to investigate the reserve funds of various banks, Xu Kan and others have completed drafting the procedural rules. These have been revised by the Standing Committee and will be submitted for approval at the second general meeting before being implemented. The detailed rules specify concrete measures for managing the reserve funds for legal tender and for the issuance and exchange of currency.

Decision to Handle Real Estate Mortgages

The Ministry of Finance, recognizing that real estate is the most significant form of collateral, and noting that its drastic price decline has affected industry and commerce, has decided to amend the regulations on real estate mortgages and establish a real estate mortgage bank to invigorate the real estate market. It is reported that the Central Trust Bureau will establish a special department for real estate mortgages, designating funds for handling real estate mortgage matters. This is because the regulations of the Central, China, and Communications Banks, as well as the Banking Law, stipulate that they cannot engage in real estate mortgage business.

Negotiable Instruments Must Be Written Using the Term "National Currency"

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday issued a notice to all members, stating, "To Whom It May Concern: We received a letter dated the 6th of this month from the Bankers Association, stating that they had received a telegram from the Tianjin Bankers Association on the 4th, stating that the Ministry of Finance has issued a nationwide order that, from the 4th of this month, the notes of the Central, China, and Communications Banks are legal tender. All transactions involving cash should comply with this order. After a joint meeting of our two associations, it was resolved that, from the 4th of this month, all negotiable instruments issued by various firms must be written using the term "National Currency." Negotiable instruments issued before this date, and those issued by customers after the 4th of this month that still use terms such as "silver dollars," "foreign silver," "silver yuan," or "foreign silver," will all be treated as "National Currency" and settled using the notes of the Central, China, and Communications Banks. In addition to sending separate letters, we are sending this special telegram to request your attention and relay this information to your esteemed Chamber of Commerce." Upon receiving this, we are issuing this notice to request your attention and compliance. With best wishes for your prosperity.

Representatives of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Grain Merchants Petition for Abolition of Bran Tax 79

Preparing Petition to Appeal to the Capital

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has appointed Zheng Zenan as its representative, along with Ying Xinyi, the national representative of the grain merchants, to petition the Fifth National Congress to abolish the additional tax on bran under the agricultural special tax in Guangdong Province. The original petition states: "Petition concerning the collection of agricultural special tax and additional tax on bran in Guangdong Province, which violates the Provisional Constitution of the Tutelage Period and the administrative order for reducing taxes, respectfully requesting that the order to abolish the tax be forwarded to uphold the legal system and benefit the people." The case was received on the 7th of this month from a joint letter from the Grain, Oil, and Cake Trade Association and the Oil Pressing Factory Trade Association, stating: "Our country is a unified nation and should have unified tax regulations. Article 62 of the Provisional Constitution of the Tutelage Period stipulates, in its third clause, against multiple taxes; in its fifth clause, against unfair taxation of goods imported from other regions for the benefit of one region; and in its sixth clause, that transit taxes on various goods should be restricted by the central government through law to avoid the following abuses. However, Guangdong Province now collects an additional tax on bran and a special tax on other agricultural products, which, according to the Provisional Constitution, should be prohibited. Regarding the additional tax on bran, in December of the 21st year of the Republic of China, the Guangdong Finance Special Commissioner's Office announced that fertilizer materials such as locally produced bean bran in Guangdong and other provinces would be exempt from additional fees. Furthermore, in May of the 23rd year, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee reiterated the order that only bean bran from the Three Eastern Provinces would be subject to fees. However, starting from September 1st of this year, the province suddenly overturned the previous administrative orders, levying a fee of 25 cents per dan on all bran, regardless of whether it is produced in the Northeast or elsewhere. This is tantamount to encouraging the import of northern products and blocking the sales of domestic products. In recent years, over twenty new oil factories have emerged in Shanghai, Hankou, Wuxi, Wujin, Kunshan, and other places. Bean cake and peanut cake produced by these factories are essential for farmers as fertilizer, and their sales volume is largest in Guangdong Province, making it a new type of industry. Now, facing this blow, it is tantamount to cutting off their livelihood. Forced to suspend operations and transportation, it has been over two months, and the impact has further pushed farmers in the bean-producing areas of eastern Henan, northern Anhui, and Shandong, as well as merchants engaged in the trading and transportation of beans and bean cakes, to the brink of ruin. Even the farmers of Guangdong Province can hardly bear this additional burden. It can truly be said that it has hundreds of harms and no benefits. This is why we must vigorously fight for the abolition of the additional tax on bran. Regarding the special tax on agricultural products, when Guangdong Province established the Agricultural Special Tax Bureau in the 18th year of the Republic of China, it was originally said that the special tax would be levied on imported agricultural products to prevent dumping. However, as a result of the tax collection, products from provinces such as Jiangsu, Shandong, Henan, Anhui, and Jiangsu were also taxed, and farmers, merchants, and transporters were restricted. This has been the case for many years. Recently, a foreign firm from a certain country transported foreign rice to Shantou, claiming a trade agreement and refusing to pay the special tax. At the same time, some people have organized a joint-stock company, hoping to transport duty-free soybean and miscellaneous grains from the Three Eastern Provinces. Under these circumstances, the so-called special tax on agricultural products may not be levied on foreign goods, while domestic grain merchants transporting soybean oil and peanut oil pay 5.4 yuan plus three commissions per dan, or 7.04 yuan in Guangdong currency. Calculating the tax rate, the tax alone is 30-40% of the value. The huge harm suffered by farmers and merchants across the country from this heavy tax on domestic products is self-evident. This is why we must vigorously fight for the abolition of the special tax on agricultural products. In short, if Guangdong Province does not immediately abolish the additional tax on domestic bran and the special tax on agricultural products, the market for bran and agricultural products in the province will be completely monopolized by foreign goods. In today's world, countries are widely implementing economic controls to prevent foreign dumping and protect their domestic industries. Guangdong Province is doing the opposite, and the harm to the national economy and the people's livelihood is not insignificant. The merchants believe that the tax system should be unified, domestic products should be protected, and the hardships of the people should be alleviated. Therefore, we have jointly requested Gu Xinyi and other representatives of the grain, oil, and cake industries from all over the country to petition the Fifth National Congress of the Chinese Nationalist Party, requesting your association to appoint a representative and prepare a separate petition to jointly appeal to the capital, striving to have the issue of the additional tax on domestic bran and the special tax on agricultural products resolved at the Fifth National Congress and a telegram sent to Guangdong Province ordering its abolition. We will be endlessly grateful." Upon receiving this, after the abolition of likin, provinces should no longer levy taxes on goods transported between them, except for customs duties. This is stipulated by the Provisional Constitution and is the administrative order that should be followed after the abolition of likin. According to estimates from the industry, this tax in Guangdong Province amounts to a massive 30-40% of the value, and it is levied in the name of taxing imported goods, but in reality, it is levied on domestic products. Even foreign merchants can resist paying, while Chinese merchants have no way to avoid it. This is even more harmful than the likin system of the past. Moreover, heavily taxing agricultural products goes against the national policy of rescuing rural areas and focusing on the people's livelihood. Over the years, merchants and the people have appealed to the government and the Guangdong authorities about this matter, but to no avail. We have no choice but to disregard the risk of intrusion and sincerely petition your esteemed association, hoping to use the party's highest power to achieve a uniform tax system and administrative orders across the country. This is how unity is maintained, and this is how farmers and merchants are benefited. Therefore, we have appointed Zheng Zenan as our representative, along with Gu Xinyi, the national representative of the grain, oil, and cake industries, to personally present the petition to your esteemed association, humbly requesting your acceptance and resolution to send a telegram to Guangdong Province ordering the abolition of the aforementioned special tax and additional tax, which would be truly beneficial to the public. Respectfully submitted to the Fifth National Congress of the Chinese Nationalist Party.

Municipal Land Bureau Plans to Draft Land Mortgage Regulations 80

Aiming to Facilitate Mortgage Convenience and Capital Circulation; Centralizing Power in Local Political Organs; First Need to Adapt the Judicial Yuan's Interpretation

Landowners in this city often mortgage their properties to banks and money lenders for business purposes to facilitate capital circulation. However, due to Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan, the auction of mortgaged property must be implemented only after a court judgment has been finalized, causing difficulties for mortgagees. It is now learned that Director Cai of the Finance Bureau, concurrently serving as Director of the Land Bureau, is making efforts to reorganize land administration, seeking ways to adapt to the needs of facts and environment and planning for flexible handling. A draft of the "Provisional Measures for Implementing Land Ownership Certificate Mortgages in Shanghai" is being submitted for approval. Whether these measures conflict with the law awaits legal experts' study. We will now present the details of these measures:

Reason: The circulation of capital in Shanghai is largely dependent on land mortgages, allowing for the borrowing of funds from banks and money lenders at any time. Banks and money lenders that accept land mortgages can easily re-mortgage them to foreign banks. Those who use title deeds to borrow from foreign banks can mortgage up to 80% of the market value of the property. However, now, even mortgaging 20% of the assessed property value is often undesirable. Although the market is experiencing tight credit and banks have too many mortgaged properties, this is one of the reasons. However, the main reason why banks are unwilling to accept mortgages is Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan, which states that to execute a mortgage, a court judgment must first be requested and finalized before an auction can be carried out. Since this interpretation, the mortgagee cannot directly auction the property when the mortgagor's debt reaches the repayment period and has not been repaid. Thus, the lending of funds lacks rapid and effective protection. To facilitate the circulation of capital and make real estate a valuable asset, it is essential to find a way to allow mortgagees to directly auction the mortgaged property when the repayment period is reached and has not been repaid, in order to provide relief. From an economic perspective, the above interpretation example cannot remain unchanged. The law should adapt to facts and environment and be changed so that it can meet the needs of society. Moreover, Article 873 of the Civil Code stipulates that the mortgagee, if the debt has reached the repayment period and has not been repaid, may apply to the court for auction of the mortgaged property and receive repayment from the proceeds. According to this provision, the exercise of mortgage rights does not require a finalized judgment. It seems that Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan is inconsistent with the original intention of Article 873 of the Civil Code. The basis of this interpretation is that the registration law and auction law have not yet been formulated, and this is not sufficient to show prudence. However, the Real Estate Registration Regulations were approved for adoption by the National Government on August 12, 1927, and the Shanghai Court continues to handle registration, still using the above-mentioned legal examples. On the one hand, registration is continued according to law, and on the other hand, the credibility of the current law is denied, which seems to undermine the dignity of the law. Moreover, the Civil Code of Property Rights Enforcement Law was promulgated by the National Government on February 10, 1930, and implemented on May 5, 1930. The Land Law, published by the National Government on June 3, 1930, in its second section, has stipulated land registration. Article 32 of the same law explains the meaning of land registration. Land registration refers to the registration of land and its fixtures, which, when compared with Article 66 and Article 758 of the Civil Code, shows that the land registration of the Land Law is the registration law mentioned in Article 3, paragraph 1 of the Civil Code of Property Rights Enforcement Law. That is, these laws and regulations have been formulated and promulgated, and the Enforcement Law has also been formulated and promulgated, but there has been no order to designate the enforcement area. The executing agency for this law is the Land Bureau, which is the land administration agency referred to in the Land Law. The Shanghai Land Bureau has been established for a long time. Since laws have been formulated and there is an agency to enforce them, if an order is issued designating Shanghai as the enforcement area, the reason that the execution of mortgage rights must be resolved through a court judgment no longer exists, and there is a considerable solution to the rapid execution of mortgage rights. As for the execution of the auction procedure, although the auction law has not been formulated, it is still prudent if the proof of legally registered rights is obtained. Even if a new auction law has not been formulated, there seems to be no need to worry excessively. Before receiving the order to designate Shanghai as the land law enforcement area, it is appropriate to draft measures to remedy the situation. The Land Bureau has long handled the registration of mortgage rights, and the registration of mortgage rights is also very cautious. Mortgage registration cannot be carried out unless the property has been surveyed, the property rights have been proven, and a land ownership certificate has been obtained at the time of setting the mortgage. Since the property rights have been proven, there is no problem. When the mortgagor fails to fulfill the contract, only the auction procedure needs to be executed, without the need for further court adjudication. This is a natural fact. However, in order to ensure fairness in the execution of the auction, the Land Bureau should send personnel to supervise it. The Land Bureau is clearer than the court regarding the land ownership restrictions in Article 14 and the use restrictions in Article 151 of the Land Law. If there is any disagreement, the Land Bureau will provide the court with the evidence of property rights and the auction situation for reference. If this is done, the interests of both the mortgagee and the mortgagor can be taken into account, and the execution of the auction procedure can be simplified. Based on these reasons, the proposed measures are as follows:

Measures: Draft of the Provisional Measures for Implementing Land Ownership Certificate Mortgages in Shanghai. Article 1: Land within this city that has been surveyed, its property rights have been proven, and a land ownership certificate has been obtained, or land that has a perpetual lease, and its mortgage rights have been registered with the Land Bureau in accordance with the Shanghai Real Estate Mortgage Registration Rules, may execute mortgage rights in accordance with these measures. Article 2: If the mortgagee's debt has reached the repayment period and has not been repaid, and the mortgagor has been urged to perform but has still not repaid, the mortgagee may directly hand over the matter to a well-known auction house in this city for execution of the auction and receive repayment from the proceeds. However, two weeks before handing over the matter to the auction house, the following items shall be reported to the Land Bureau: 1. The registration number of the mortgage, as well as the date of its registration. 2. Proof that performance has been urged after the repayment period has expired. 3. The name of the auction house and the date of the auction. The aforementioned auction house shall report its capital amount and business status to the Land Bureau for registration, and the registration regulations shall be determined separately. Article 3: When mortgaged property is auctioned, the mortgagee shall apply to the Land Bureau to send personnel to supervise the proceedings. Article 4: If the mortgagor disagrees with the implementation of the auction of the mortgaged property, before the establishment of the Land Tribunal, all evidence of the establishment of the mortgage and the evidence of urging performance of the debt shall be transferred to the court for immediate review. However, after the establishment of the Land Tribunal, it shall be reviewed by the Land Tribunal. The aforementioned appeal shall not suspend the implementation, but in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of these Measures, the mortgagee shall be ordered to provide a guarantee of a considerable amount. Article 5: If there are special circumstances and it is necessary to order the mortgagee to provide a guarantee, with the approval of the Director of the Land Bureau, the mortgagee shall be ordered to provide a considerable guarantee as a condition for implementing the auction. The aforementioned guarantee may be provided in the form of a reputable store, valuable securities, or cash. However, if a store guarantee is used, a balance sheet of assets and liabilities that has been certified by an accountant and the Chamber of Commerce shall be submitted to the Land Bureau for filing along with the guarantee. Article 6: For land auctioned in accordance with these Measures, the purchaser shall go to the Land Bureau with the mortgagee and apply for transfer in accordance with Article 6 of the Real Estate Mortgage Registration Rules, and the mortgage registration shall be cancelled. However, the transfer of perpetual lease land shall be handled in accordance with the established regulations. Article 7: For land where mortgage rights have been established, if there are other disputes besides disagreement with the implementation of the auction, the litigation procedure shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 4, paragraph 1 of these Measures. Article 8: If the mortgagee loses the lawsuit after the litigation procedure in Article 4 of these Measures is finalized, and the other party has suffered losses, the guarantee or valuable securities provided in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 and Article 5 of these Measures shall be used to compensate for the losses. However, if the guarantee is provided by a store, the store shall be jointly and severally liable for compensation. Article 9: These Measures shall be implemented upon approval by the National Government.

Aviation Mobile Exhibition Opens in Southern District Today 81

Venue is the Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road

Guomin News reports that the Shanghai Solicitation Headquarters of the Chinese Aviation Association is preparing to hold an aviation mobile exhibition to give citizens a deep understanding of aviation for national salvation and air defense knowledge. The city is divided into five areas: Southern Shanghai, Northern Shanghai, Pudong, Western Shanghai, and the Special District, to be held sequentially. Preparations for the Southern Shanghai exhibition have been completed, and it has been decided to officially open today (10th) at 10:00 AM at the Public Education Center on Wenmiao Road, with a planned exhibition period of ten days.

Models and Photos

In addition to collecting dozens of types of aircraft models and photos with explanations, the exhibition will also publicly display the association's establishment process and photos of the public's donations for purchasing aircraft. In addition, a large bamboo shed will be built in front of the auditorium, and the Jiangfeng aircraft manufactured by the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant will be transported there for display.

Slogans and Items

The association has specially produced many enameled slogan signs and posted them in the exhibition hall, such as "Aviation is a Vanguard for National Salvation, Strive to Build Aviation, Strive to Develop Civil Aviation, National Difficulties Cannot Be Resolved Without Building Aviation" and "Aviation Saves the Nation." The exhibits are divided into two rooms. In addition to the Naval Department's Jiangfeng aircraft, there are also eighteen aircraft models, including the Wuzi water training aircraft, the Bingzi military aircraft, the Curtiss Focke-Wulf seaplane fighter, the Consolidated bomber, the Curtiss Hawk fighter, the Yizi seaplane reconnaissance and training aircraft, the Haiying and Jianghe aircraft.

Scattering Leaflets

In order to widely recruit members and make it easier for the general public to join the society, the Chinese Flying Society has specially set up a temporary registration office at the Public Education Center during the aviation exhibition period. At the same time, the aviation mobile exhibition has agreed with the airline to use airplanes to fly in the sky and scatter a large number of leaflets to expand publicity.

Discussing Pacific Shipping Routes and Trade Issues, Sino-American Association Sends Du Huisheng as Representative

The Pacific Foreign Trade Association will hold its 12th annual meeting in Honolulu on the 27th of this month to discuss Pacific shipping routes and foreign trade issues. The Western American Chamber of Commerce will also hold its annual meeting in Honolulu at the same time, and has sent letters inviting the Sino-American Trade Association, the China International Trade Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and other organizations to send representatives to attend. It is now known that the Sino-American Association has appointed Du Huisheng, the honorary representative of the China International Trade Association in Honolulu, to attend as its representative. The incoming letters and discussion proposals are recorded below:

Invitation to Participate

Respectfully, we hereby issue an invitation to all business circles, especially members of various commercial organizations and groups, to take the opportunity of traveling to the United States this autumn and respectfully attend the 12th annual meeting of the Pacific Foreign Trade Association. This meeting is designed for all business circles concerned about the progress of trade in countries on the west coast of the Pacific. It will be held in Honolulu from November 27th to 30th. At that time, various chambers of commerce in the western United States will also be held in that port. At this time of world economic turmoil, it is to convene business circles from countries across the Pacific to jointly discuss how to deal with the current changing situation. Honolulu is geographically the most suitable point for Pacific transportation. Business leaders can gather together to exchange opinions. From the American point of view, business leaders can take this opportunity to gather together to seek ways to improve Pacific trade, and how to express their great theories on foreign policy. Our association makes this meeting an expanded nature, bringing together American merchants and merchants from countries along the Pacific coast to jointly observe and study, and all trade problems in the future may be solved easily. Merchants from all countries, whether they come to Honolulu to participate in the meeting or not, can send their great theories for discussion. The meeting is not far away, please proceed early and select representatives to inform us by letter so that they can be included in the meeting schedule. Please send submissions to "Committee of the Pacific Trade Association via the Honolulu Chamber of Commerce of the United States". Please also indicate the travel schedule as soon as possible so that we can welcome you. Sincerely, Chairman of the Pacific Foreign Trade Association. (2) Respectfully, the Western American Chamber of Commerce holds a meeting once a year to discuss various important industrial and commercial issues. Chambers of commerce and business organizations in the West send representatives to participate. This year's meeting will be held in Honolulu from November 27th to 30th. The Pacific Trade Association is holding its 12th annual meeting at this time. Our association and the Pacific Trade Association and others hope that business circles in your country, especially the members of the council, will take the opportunity to travel to the United States and attend the meeting, which is limited to glory. Business leaders gather here, and the trade association will make many contributions. When arriving in port, you can first notify Mr. Leonard F. Pead, the business manager of the Western American Chamber of Commerce at the Hawaiian Nairo Hotel in Honolulu, so that you can participate in various meetings. Sincerely, Vice President of the American Chamber of Commerce

Discussion Proposals

The Pacific Trade Association will discuss the following matters: (1) Trade barriers, restrictions and obstacles regarding shipping, cargo, passengers and transportation.

(2) Reciprocal Trade Agreements, review of draft reciprocal trade agreements between countries along the west coast of the Pacific. (3) Exchange Rate Fluctuations, methods to stabilize exchange rates and remedy them, and the establishment of independent credit institutions to stabilize international trade. (4) Other matters, regarding the exchange of goods and the reduction of trade barriers, as well as issues such as transportation and trade trends. The four American Chambers of Commerce will discuss the following matters: (1) Pacific airline routes and foreign trade, (2) Pacific trade trends, (3) Stabilization of exchange rates, (4) Overview of Pacific lumber exports, (5) Pacific trade policy, (6) The future of the Philippines in Pacific trade, (7) The impact of British preferential tax rates on the Pacific, (8) The problem of American ocean merchants, (9) Transportation issues across the Pacific, (10) Reciprocal trade agreements and Pacific trade.

Zhejiang Public Association Held a Board Meeting Yesterday 84

Chairman Chu Huiseng Resolved Important Cases, Recommended the Ministry of Industry to Prepare for the Establishment of a Special School for Aquatic Products

The Zhejiang Public Association held its first board meeting at its clubhouse on Avenue Edward VII at 6 pm last night. More than 40 people attended. Chu Huiseng was publicly elected as chairman. After the chairman reported on the association's affairs, the agenda was discussed and the Ministry of Industry was recommended to establish a fisheries school. The details are recorded as follows:

Resolved Cases

(1) Improving tobacco leaves: It was resolved that the association should prepare funds to purchase seeds from the United States and distribute them to tobacco-producing areas in the province for trial planting. Dai Gengxin, Wu Wenyuan, Hua Zhenxin, Hu Yangqian, Wu Guochang, Pan Zhijiang, and Yu Hualong were publicly elected as members of the committee for improving domestic tobacco leaves. (2) Omitted. (3) It was resolved to recommend that the government dredge the Cao'e River as soon as possible. (4) (5) The chairman committee was designated as Chu Huiseng, Wang Ji, and Yin Zhufu. The standing committee members were Cha Zhongjian, Xu Dafu, Shen Hengshan, Zhuang Yuqing, Zhang Shenzhi, Wei Bozheng, Shen Tianxin, Yu Zhongxian, Wu Gecang, Yu Hualong, Hu Fengxiang, Xu Xiajun, Jiang Zhongquan, He Dekui, Shen Huachen, Zhu Meixian, and 17 others. (6) It was resolved to submit a request to recommend that the Ministry of Industry prepare for the establishment of a national vocational school for aquatic products, and to restore the Zhejiang Dinghai Fisheries School, and to establish branch schools in coastal provinces.

Original Recommendation

Respectfully, our association, in order to revitalize fisheries education, resolved at a general meeting of members to recommend that the Ministry of Industry prepare for the establishment of a national vocational school for aquatic products, and to restore the Zhejiang Dinghai Fisheries School, and to establish branch schools in coastal provinces. A telegram was sent to the Ministry of Industry, stating, "It is found that all countries in the East and West are actively expanding the development of aquatic education. For example, the Netherlands, a small country, has as many as 30 fisheries schools. Japan's fisheries education is almost all over the country, in order to expand its inherent production and develop its future treasures. Our country's territorial waters are vast, from the Bohai Sea to the South China Sea, and the coastline stretches for tens of thousands of miles. Aquatic tribes thrive, and shellfish scales can be taken endlessly. If there are large-scale academic groups to conduct research and practice on new fishing methods and swimming techniques, as well as the driving of wheeled ships, so that fishermen can have sufficient knowledge and skills, the progress of our country's fisheries will be unlimited. However, due to the weakness of fishermen's abilities and the immaturity of their level, they stick to old habits and do not think about progress. There is also no strong unity and novel fishing nets, so they cannot cross the ocean and only carry out old-fashioned fishing in the near sea, which makes foreign fishing boats frequently appear in Chinese waters, fishing across borders. The fish delicacies popular on the market, such as shark fins, sea cucumbers, squid, abalone, scallops, etc., and second-class products such as salmon, etc., mostly come from imported products. The loss of maritime power and the outflow of loopholes are regrettable. Moreover, our country's sea surface is vast, with lurking bandits and latent threats. Fishermen are afraid of traveling far overseas. Often, after sailing hundreds of miles, they do not see a neighboring ship passing or docking. The vast sea is deserted. Pirates are rampant and tourists are increasingly frightened. Therefore, if we want to ensure maritime safety, we must first seek the progress of fisheries. At a distance of ten or twenty miles from the sea or on the side of uninhabited barren islands, there must be a number of fishing boats gathered in it, so that pirates will be afraid and change their careers. Therefore, the development of fisheries is not only about developing profit sources, but also about consolidating the sea. The only way to develop fisheries is to promote aquatic education. Our country's aquatic education only has the Jiangsu Chongming Fisheries School. The Zhejiang Dinghai Fisheries School was established in the fifth year of the Republic of China and was closed last autumn due to disputes over changes in leadership. Guangdong is still in the process of preparation. With the vast territory of our country's territorial waters and millions of fishermen along the coast, there is only one fisheries school in the country, which is not enough to meet the needs of researching aquatic education, and to revitalize domestic industry and open up solid profit sources. The Ministry of Industry has recently set up a fishing market in Shanghai with a large amount of money, which is in line with the purpose. It is proposed to consider that fisheries are an important production industry in the coastal area, and a special amount of money should be allocated to prepare for the establishment of a national vocational school for aquatic products. The address should be set in the disputed Shengsi Islands on the border between Jiangsu and Zhejiang, where fishermen gather. On the one hand, the Zhejiang Dinghai Fisheries School should be restored, and branch schools should be established in coastal provinces. The original schools in Jiangsu and Zhejiang should also be renamed branch schools in order to unify and assign special responsibilities. This matter concerns the training of national fisheries talents and has been fully approved by the general meeting of members of our association. For this reason, a telegram is sent, requesting that the Ministry carefully review and select it for implementation," and decided to send letters to the county party headquarters and various legal entities to unanimously advocate for it. A corresponding letter is sent to your party headquarters for your reference and to inform the various legal entities in your county, hoping that you will give it your sympathy and assistance.

Silver Shops Allowed by the Government to Purchase Grade A Silver Bars for Raw Materials 87

National Conference Suspended

The National News Agency reporter met Mr. Fu Shengmao, chairman of the Silver Shops Association, yesterday and asked about the industry's request for the government to interpret the use of silver for raw materials. According to him, he visited a responsible person from a government agency for this issue. According to his informal statement, the government will facilitate the raw material problem of silver shops and allow the purchase of Grade A silver bars for melting to make utensils. Because there are two types of silver bars, Grade A and Grade B. Grade A silver bars, also known as 39 silver bars, mean that each hundred taels contains 99 taels and 9 qian of pure silver. Grade B silver bars, also known as 88 silver bars, mean that each hundred taels contains 88 taels of silver. In addition to making silver coins, the country specially made this kind of 39 silver bars for the purpose of making utensils. In the future, this kind of silver bars can be purchased from the Central Bank. As for customers, if they exchange old jewelry, they can also be accepted because their color is still 39, so it does not violate the government's policy of silver nationalization. Therefore, our industry is still operating as usual. The national conference that was originally planned to be convened has also been suspended.

Municipal Federation Suggests to the Municipal Council 95

Four Methods to Solve the Telephone Price Increase Problem

The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation sent a letter to the Municipal Council yesterday regarding the telephone price increase, proposing four solutions. The original text reads, "Respectfully, since the Shanghai Telephone Company, in the face of the sluggish market situation, recklessly hoped to satisfy its desire for an annual interest rate of one point, and issued a ridiculous move to demand a price increase, public opinion unanimously expressed opposition. Fortunately, your bureau took into account the difficulties of the times and the burden on users, so it specially invited experts to review it and solemnly handled the matter. We are very grateful. Unexpectedly, the expert research results favored one side. In its report, it even recognized the company's request for an annual interest rate of one point as correct, and offered advice to charge by the number of calls as a disguised price increase, while completely ignoring the company's wasteful expenses, the wrong interest rate, and whether users can afford it. All circles have expressed indignation at this. We believe that the telephone is a public utility and a communication tool, and should strive to be common, with low fees and many installations as the principle. Even if the company is concerned about business, it should also profit from the increase, otherwise, the more the telephone fee increases, the fewer users there will be, and as a result, the company will inevitably fail. Now, in the expert report, the regulations on the charging by the number of calls are: 10 yuan per month for stores, which can make 150 calls, and 6 yuan and 5 jiao per month for households, which can make 100 calls. For any number exceeding the above, a fee of 3 cents will be charged for each call. From the surface, the monthly rent seems to be slightly lower than before, but due to the strict restrictions on the number of calls and the high fees for exceeding the number, the burden on users has actually increased significantly. Therefore, if the expert's opinion is implemented rashly, users will be forced to remove them due to the heavy telephone fees, and the company will not only not be able to achieve its extravagant hope of an annual interest rate of one point, but will also be in a more difficult situation. It can be boldly asserted that our association will also conduct careful discussions, believing that even if the charging by the number of calls method is to be implemented, it should be amended as follows: (1) The monthly rent should be reduced to 6 yuan for stores and 3 yuan for households. (2) The basic number of calls should be increased to 300 per month for stores and 200 for residences. (3) A fee of 2 cents should be charged for each call exceeding the number. (4) The call fee between the urban area and the special area should be cancelled. In this way, fairness can be seen, and there will be fewer obstacles in the implementation of the charging by the number of calls method. On the one hand, due to the reduction in telephone fees, it will inevitably attract an increase in users. This will definitely promote the development of the company's business. The special zone telephone problem will be the final decision of your bureau, so we are submitting our opinions for your adoption, which will benefit both users and the company."

Hong Kong National Bank Shanghai Branch Creditors' Committee Bankruptcy Petition Rejected 96

And Ordered to Bear Litigation Costs

Lawyer Liang Yaobing, formerly in the name of the Hong Kong National Bank Shanghai Branch Creditors' Committee, filed a case with the First Special District Court to declare the branch bankrupt. The court rejected the case and ordered the committee to bear the litigation costs. The reasons for the ruling are recorded as follows: Bankruptcy is declared when a debtor is unable to pay off their debts. Furthermore, if a debtor ceases payment, it is presumed that they are unable to pay, as clearly stipulated in Articles 50 and 1, Paragraph 2 of the Bankruptcy Law. However, the so-called cessation of payment in Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the law, which presumes inability to pay, allows the debtor to legally present evidence to refute this presumption. In this case, the petitioner, entrusted by the creditors, petitioned for a declaration of bankruptcy on behalf of creditors with common interests. Although the lawsuit is not inherently illegal, the reason for the bankruptcy petition is solely that the debtor announced a business closure on September 16th of this year, ceasing payments. According to Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Bankruptcy Law, this should be presumed as an inability to pay. Therefore, according to the provisions of Articles 57 and 58, Paragraph 1 of the same law, the petitioner requested a declaration of bankruptcy for the debtor. The petition is based entirely on the presumed fact of inability to pay. However, the debtor has presented an audit report from accountant Wang Zikang, proving that the debtor's assets are sufficient to cover its debts with a surplus. Furthermore, the newspaper clipping submitted by the petitioner (Exhibit 1) also contains a statement from their representative lawyer, Liang Yaobing, to reporters, stating that the situation of the National Bank in Shanghai is relatively good, and its assets exceed its liabilities. This is sufficient evidence that the debtor's assets are indeed sufficient to pay off its debts. The petitioner's sudden petition for a declaration of bankruptcy is not legally sound and should be rejected. In accordance with Article 5 of the Bankruptcy Law and Articles 95 and 78 of the Code of Civil Procedure, the ruling is as stated in the main text.

Tenant Forced into Rent Arrears Commits Suicide by Drinking Nitric Acid 97

Li Wenbin's Business Failure: How Does the Landlord Feel About This?

Li Wenbin, a native of Wuxi (45 years old), residing at No. 9, Lane 46, Meijia Lane in this city, formerly ran a copper workshop. Recently, due to business failure, he ceased operations, and his life fell into dire straits. Recently, his landlord, Shen Xie Jia, filed a lawsuit in the local court, requesting the recovery of rent arrears and the eviction of the tenant. The court ruled that Li Wenbin should pay 196 yuan in rent arrears and vacate the premises within a specified period. Li expressed his willingness to vacate, but requested that the landlord allow him to pay the rent arrears in installments, which the landlord refused. Li, in a moment of desperation, conceived a suicidal idea. He secretly swallowed nitric acid the night before. When the poison took effect and he began to moan, his family discovered him and immediately sent him to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died. The hospital sent the body to the coroner's office. Yesterday, after the court confirmed the cause of death, the family retrieved the body and placed it in a coffin at home.

Wang's wife, Chen (43 years old), lives in the factory. Yesterday afternoon, at around 3:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the factory. Because varnish is extremely flammable, sparks flew everywhere in an instant, affecting the entire house and piercing through the roof. At the time, Wang and his wife were upstairs. Fortunately, the fire brigade had received a report at this time and rushed to the scene, and the fire was extinguished with great effort. However, neighboring houses had been affected. An ambulance was immediately used to send the injured to the hospital. Wang Youlin eventually died of his injuries at 5:30 PM. The police were notified, and the body was transferred to the coroner's office for examination while investigating the cause of the fire to serve as a basis for handling the matter.

Notorious Pickpocket Sentenced 101

Enticing a Young Girl for Attempted Rape Revealed the Crime: Hu Asheng, Xu Decai, and Others Suffer Punishment

Xu Decai, a native of Qingjiang, known as "Big Head Xu," a master pickpocket in Shanghai, and Hu Asheng, a native of Ningbo, had many accomplices under their command. They specialized in performing their sleight-of-hand skills in streetcars, movie theaters, and other places in the British, French, and Chinese sections, and had never been caught. In this line of work, the jargon is called "hard pickpocketing," also known as "running a dying business." This time, however, they were destined to be caught. The reason is that on the afternoon of the 14th of last month, Hu Asheng lured a fellow villager, Wang Xiaocai (16 years old), to Room 342 of the Dafang Hotel on Zhengjia Wood Bridge, intending to rape her. After the girl managed to escape, Hu, feeling resentful for having wasted the room money, reported to the French Police, claiming that Wang Xiaocai had swindled him out of five yuan in prostitution money and stolen thirty yuan in foreign currency before fleeing. The police chief approved the report and sent detectives to investigate. After questioning Wang, they learned that Hu had made a false accusation out of spite. After a thorough investigation by Detective Lu Zhulin and Detective Zhu Zhihao, they discovered that Hu and Xu were notorious pickpockets. They arrested Hu and also arrested Xu and his accomplices Wang Dehua, Yuan Hailin, etc., and sent them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. The details have already been reported. Subsequently, the police discovered that Hu, Xu, and others had committed hundreds of theft cases in the concession, but very few victims had been notified to come to court. The reason is that it was impossible to notify most of them. The case was prosecuted by the Police Department in accordance with the law. Judge Wang Gangxu, the head of the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, repeatedly opened court sessions to hear and examine the case and declared the debate concluded. He found that Yuan Hailin had engaged in receiving and selling stolen goods, and ordered him to post bail and await sentencing. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. In the afternoon, Judge Wang came to the Second Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to be brought to the court. Hu Asheng was sentenced to three years of imprisonment for jointly committing continuous theft. Xu Decai (same charge) was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment. Yuan Hailin was fined 60 yuan; if he chose to perform labor in lieu of payment, it would be calculated at one yuan per day. Wang Dehua was found not guilty. During the appeal period, Hu and Xu were ordered to be detained in the detention center, Yuan was released on his original bail, and Wang was released on 500 yuan bail guaranteeing his availability for questioning at any time; if he could not provide bail, he would be detained.

Silk Trade Discusses Price Increase 102

The Shanghai Silk Trade Association, Qianjiang Guild Hall, Crepe Trade Association, Shengjing Guild Hall, and other silk trade organizations convened an emergency meeting of all member firms at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss the issue of silk prices. Since the government implemented the legal tender system, material prices have soared. Raw silk was only about 350 yuan per load in early autumn, and has gradually increased to nearly 900 yuan. Furthermore, foreign firms are aggressively buying up silk, resulting in a shortage of fine silk supply, which has greatly increased costs. To maintain production costs, it is necessary to discuss solutions. The meeting resulted in a decision to notify all firms that, effective immediately, all pure silk woven goods will have a temporary price increase of 5% and rayon-silk woven goods will have a temporary price increase of 3% to maintain costs. The discussion continued until evening before adjourning.
